<a href="#4575"><div id="4574">1.</div></a>
<a href="#4576"><div id="4575">Simultaneous</div></a>
<a href="#4577"><div id="4576">localization</div></a>
<a href="#4578"><div id="4577">and</div></a>
<a href="#4579"><div id="4578">mapping</div></a>
<a href="#4580"><div id="4579">(SLAM): SLAM</div></a>
<a href="#4581"><div id="4580">is</div></a>
<a href="#4582"><div id="4581">a</div></a>
<a href="#4583"><div id="4582">type</div></a>
<a href="#4584"><div id="4583">of</div></a>
<a href="#4585"><div id="4584">algorithm</div></a>
<a href="#4586"><div id="4585">that</div></a>
<a href="#4587"><div id="4586">enables</div></a>
<a href="#4588"><div id="4587">a</div></a>
<a href="#4589"><div id="4588">measurement</div></a>
<a href="#4590"><div id="4589">unit</div></a>
<a href="#4591"><div id="4590">(typically</div></a>
<a href="#4592"><div id="4591">a</div></a>
<a href="#4593"><div id="4592">mobile</div></a>
<a href="#4594"><div id="4593">robot)</div></a>
<a href="#4595"><div id="4594">to</div></a>
<a href="#4596"><div id="4595">generate</div></a>
<a href="#4597"><div id="4596">a</div></a>
<a href="#4598"><div id="4597">map</div></a>
<a href="#4599"><div id="4598">of</div></a>
<a href="#4600"><div id="4599">its</div></a>
<a href="#4601"><div id="4600">surroundings</div></a>
<a href="#4602"><div id="4601">and</div></a>
<a href="#4603"><div id="4602">its</div></a>
<a href="#4604"><div id="4603">position</div></a>
<a href="#4605"><div id="4604">in</div></a>
<a href="#4606"><div id="4605">this</div></a>
<a href="#4607"><div id="4606">map</div></a>
<a href="#4608"><div id="4607">at</div></a>
<a href="#4609"><div id="4608">the</div></a>
<a href="#4610"><div id="4609">same</div></a>
<a href="#4611"><div id="4610">time.</div></a>
<a href="#4612"><div id="4611">This</div></a>
<a href="#4613"><div id="4612">method</div></a>
<a href="#4614"><div id="4613">assumes</div></a>
<a href="#4615"><div id="4614">that,</div></a>
<a href="#4616"><div id="4615">as</div></a>
<a href="#4617"><div id="4616">a</div></a>
<a href="#4618"><div id="4617">measurement</div></a>
<a href="#4619"><div id="4618">unit</div></a>
<a href="#4620"><div id="4619">repeatedly</div></a>
<a href="#4621"><div id="4620">passes</div></a>
<a href="#4622"><div id="4621">by</div></a>

<a href="#4624"><div id="4623">set</div></a>
<a href="#4625"><div id="4624">of</div></a>
<a href="#4626"><div id="4625">features,</div></a>

<a href="#4628"><div id="4627">is</div></a>
<a href="#4629"><div id="4628">possible</div></a>
<a href="#4630"><div id="4629">use</div></a>
<a href="#4631"><div id="4630">these</div></a>
<a href="#4632"><div id="4631">features</div></a>
<a href="#4633"><div id="4632">as</div></a>
<a href="#4634"><div id="4633">referencing</div></a>
<a href="#4635"><div id="4634">points,</div></a>
<a href="#4636"><div id="4635">based</div></a>
<a href="#4637"><div id="4636">on</div></a>
<a href="#4638"><div id="4637">which</div></a>
<a href="#4639"><div id="4638">an</div></a>
<a href="#4640"><div id="4639">algorithm</div></a>
<a href="#4641"><div id="4640">can</div></a>
<a href="#4642"><div id="4641">update</div></a>
<a href="#4643"><div id="4642">the</div></a>
<a href="#4644"><div id="4643">position</div></a>
<a href="#4645"><div id="4644">estimate.</div></a>
<a href="#4646"><div id="4645">In</div></a>
<a href="#4647"><div id="4646">particular,</div></a>
<a href="#4648"><div id="4647">the</div></a>
<a href="#4649"><div id="4648">algorithm</div></a>
<a href="#4650"><div id="4649">takes</div></a>
<a href="#4651"><div id="4650">in</div></a>
<a href="#4652"><div id="4651">sensor</div></a>
<a href="#4653"><div id="4652">measurements,</div></a>
<a href="#4654"><div id="4653">predicts</div></a>
<a href="#4655"><div id="4654">the</div></a>
<a href="#4656"><div id="4655">expected</div></a>
<a href="#4657"><div id="4656">position</div></a>
<a href="#4658"><div id="4657">and</div></a>
<a href="#4659"><div id="4658">sensor</div></a>
<a href="#4660"><div id="4659">measurement,</div></a>
<a href="#4661"><div id="4660">compares</div></a>
<a href="#4662"><div id="4661">the</div></a>
<a href="#4663"><div id="4662">predicted</div></a>
<a href="#4664"><div id="4663">measurements</div></a>
<a href="#4665"><div id="4664">with</div></a>
<a href="#4666"><div id="4665">the</div></a>
<a href="#4667"><div id="4666">actual</div></a>
<a href="#4668"><div id="4667">measurements,</div></a>
<a href="#4669"><div id="4668">and</div></a>
<a href="#4670"><div id="4669">uses</div></a>
<a href="#4671"><div id="4670">the</div></a>
<a href="#4672"><div id="4671">error</div></a>
<a href="#4673"><div id="4672">to</div></a>
<a href="#4674"><div id="4673">update</div></a>
<a href="#4675"><div id="4674">the</div></a>
<a href="#4676"><div id="4675">position</div></a>
<a href="#4677"><div id="4676">prediction</div></a>
<a href="#4678"><div id="4677">algorithm.</div></a>
<a href="#4679"><div id="4678">2.</div></a>
<a href="#4680"><div id="4679">Range-based</div></a>
<a href="#4681"><div id="4680">algorithms:</div></a>
<a href="#4682"><div id="4681">a.</div></a>

<a href="#4684"><div id="4683">of</div></a>
<a href="#4685"><div id="4684">flight:</div></a>
<a href="#4686"><div id="4685">the</div></a>
<a href="#4687"><div id="4686">algorithm</div></a>
<a href="#4688"><div id="4687">measures</div></a>
<a href="#4689"><div id="4688">the</div></a>
<a href="#4690"><div id="4689">propagation</div></a>

<a href="#4692"><div id="4691">of</div></a>
<a href="#4693"><div id="4692">a</div></a>

<a href="#4695"><div id="4694">between</div></a>

<a href="#4698"><div id="4697">and</div></a>
<a href="#4699"><div id="4698">the</div></a>

<a href="#4705"><div id="4704">by</div></a>

<a href="#4708"><div id="4707">of</div></a>
<a href="#4709"><div id="4708">signal</div></a>

<a href="#4711"><div id="4710">estimate</div></a>

<a href="#4713"><div id="4712">distance</div></a>
<a href="#4714"><div id="4713">between</div></a>
<a href="#4715"><div id="4714">the</div></a>
<a href="#4716"><div id="4715">transmitter</div></a>
<a href="#4717"><div id="4716">and</div></a>
<a href="#4718"><div id="4717">the</div></a>
<a href="#4719"><div id="4718">receiver.</div></a>

<a href="#4722"><div id="4721">based</div></a>

<a href="#4725"><div id="4724">algorithm</div></a>

<a href="#4728"><div id="4727">angle</div></a>

<a href="#4745"><div id="4744">3.</div></a>

<a href="#4747"><div id="4746">signal</div></a>

<a href="#4750"><div id="4749">measures</div></a>

<a href="#4752"><div id="4751">received</div></a>

<a href="#4780"><div id="4779">4.</div></a>
<a href="#4781"><div id="4780">Range-free:</div></a>
<a href="#4782"><div id="4781">a.</div></a>
<a href="#4783"><div id="4782">Proximity:</div></a>
<a href="#4784"><div id="4783">the</div></a>
<a href="#4785"><div id="4784">algorithm</div></a>
<a href="#4786"><div id="4785">checks</div></a>
<a href="#4787"><div id="4786">if</div></a>
<a href="#4788"><div id="4787">the</div></a>
<a href="#4789"><div id="4788">user’s</div></a>
<a href="#4790"><div id="4789">device</div></a>
<a href="#4791"><div id="4790">is</div></a>
<a href="#4792"><div id="4791">connected</div></a>
<a href="#4793"><div id="4792">to</div></a>
<a href="#4794"><div id="4793">any</div></a>
<a href="#4795"><div id="4794">beacons</div></a>

<a href="#4802"><div id="4801">this</div></a>
<a href="#4803"><div id="4802">connectivity</div></a>
<a href="#4804"><div id="4803">data,</div></a>

<a href="#4808"><div id="4807">of</div></a>
<a href="#4809"><div id="4808">the</div></a>
<a href="#4810"><div id="4809">user.</div></a>
<a href="#4811"><div id="4810">(See</div></a>
<a href="#4812"><div id="4811">Fig.</div></a>
<a href="#4813"><div id="4812">3.1)</div></a>
<a href="#4814"><div id="4813">b.</div></a>
<a href="#4815"><div id="4814">Fingerprinting:</div></a>
<a href="#4816"><div id="4815">the</div></a>
<a href="#4817"><div id="4816">algorithm</div></a>
<a href="#4818"><div id="4817">measures</div></a>
<a href="#4819"><div id="4818">signals</div></a>
<a href="#4820"><div id="4819">received</div></a>

<a href="#4828"><div id="4827">received</div></a>
<a href="#4829"><div id="4828">data</div></a>

<a href="#4833"><div id="4832">in</div></a>
<a href="#4834"><div id="4833">the</div></a>
<a href="#4835"><div id="4834">database,</div></a>
<a href="#4836"><div id="4835">and</div></a>
<a href="#4837"><div id="4836">selects</div></a>

<a href="#4842"><div id="4841">the</div></a>
<a href="#4843"><div id="4842">database</div></a>
<a href="#4844"><div id="4843">that</div></a>
<a href="#4845"><div id="4844">best</div></a>

<a href="#4847"><div id="4846">the</div></a>
<a href="#4848"><div id="4847">received</div></a>

<a href="#4853"><div id="4852">Widely-Used</div></a>

<a href="#4855"><div id="4854">Technologies</div></a>

<a href="#4862"><div id="4861">ranged-based</div></a>

<a href="#4871"><div id="4870">algorithm</div></a>

<a href="#4877"><div id="4876">a</div></a>

<a href="#4881"><div id="4880">a</div></a>
<a href="#4882"><div id="4881">WiFi</div></a>
<a href="#4883"><div id="4882">router.</div></a>
<a href="#4884"><div id="4883">The</div></a>
<a href="#4885"><div id="4884">main</div></a>
<a href="#4886"><div id="4885">advantages</div></a>
<a href="#4887"><div id="4886">of</div></a>

<a href="#4890"><div id="4889">system</div></a>
<a href="#4891"><div id="4890">are</div></a>
<a href="#4892"><div id="4891">wide-reception</div></a>
<a href="#4893"><div id="4892">range,</div></a>
<a href="#4894"><div id="4893">low</div></a>
<a href="#4895"><div id="4894">cost</div></a>

<a href="#4899"><div id="4898">energy</div></a>
<a href="#4900"><div id="4899">consumption,</div></a>
<a href="#4901"><div id="4900">and</div></a>
<a href="#4902"><div id="4901">device</div></a>
<a href="#4903"><div id="4902">availability.</div></a>
<a href="#4904"><div id="4903">In</div></a>
<a href="#4905"><div id="4904">particular,</div></a>
<a href="#4906"><div id="4905">almost</div></a>
<a href="#4907"><div id="4906">every</div></a>
<a href="#4908"><div id="4907">mobile</div></a>
<a href="#4909"><div id="4908">phone</div></a>
<a href="#4910"><div id="4909">is</div></a>
<a href="#4911"><div id="4910">equipped</div></a>
<a href="#4912"><div id="4911">with</div></a>
<a href="#4913"><div id="4912">WiFi</div></a>
<a href="#4914"><div id="4913">connection,</div></a>
<a href="#4915"><div id="4914">and</div></a>
<a href="#4916"><div id="4915">thus</div></a>
<a href="#4917"><div id="4916">the</div></a>
<a href="#4918"><div id="4917">visitors</div></a>
<a href="#4919"><div id="4918">to</div></a>
<a href="#4920"><div id="4919">a</div></a>
<a href="#4921"><div id="4920">museum</div></a>
<a href="#4922"><div id="4921">do</div></a>
<a href="#4923"><div id="4922">not</div></a>
<a href="#4924"><div id="4923">have</div></a>
<a href="#4925"><div id="4924">to</div></a>
<a href="#4926"><div id="4925">carry</div></a>
<a href="#4927"><div id="4926">extra</div></a>
<a href="#4928"><div id="4927">devices</div></a>
<a href="#4929"><div id="4928">on</div></a>

<a href="#4933"><div id="4932">WiFi-based</div></a>
<a href="#4934"><div id="4933">navigation</div></a>
<a href="#4935"><div id="4934">technology.</div></a>
<a href="#4936"><div id="4935">The</div></a>
<a href="#4937"><div id="4936">main</div></a>
<a href="#4938"><div id="4937">disadvantages</div></a>
<a href="#4939"><div id="4938">of</div></a>
<a href="#4940"><div id="4939">WiFi</div></a>
<a href="#4941"><div id="4940">localization</div></a>
<a href="#4942"><div id="4941">system</div></a>
<a href="#4943"><div id="4942">are</div></a>
<a href="#4944"><div id="4943">installation</div></a>
<a href="#4945"><div id="4944">difficulty,</div></a>
<a href="#4946"><div id="4945">poor</div></a>
<a href="#4947"><div id="4946">distance</div></a>
<a href="#4948"><div id="4947">measurement</div></a>
<a href="#4949"><div id="4948">accuracy,</div></a>
<a href="#4950"><div id="4949">and</div></a>
<a href="#4951"><div id="4950">requirement</div></a>
<a href="#4952"><div id="4951">of</div></a>
<a href="#4953"><div id="4952">complex</div></a>
<a href="#4954"><div id="4953">signal</div></a>
<a href="#4955"><div id="4954">processing</div></a>
<a href="#4956"><div id="4955">algorithms.</div></a>
<a href="#4957"><div id="4956">It</div></a>
<a href="#4958"><div id="4957">typically</div></a>
<a href="#4959"><div id="4958">takes</div></a>
<a href="#4960"><div id="4959">an</div></a>
<a href="#4961"><div id="4960">entire</div></a>
<a href="#4962"><div id="4961">research</div></a>
<a href="#4963"><div id="4962">team</div></a>
<a href="#4964"><div id="4963">to</div></a>
<a href="#4965"><div id="4964">build</div></a>
<a href="#4966"><div id="4965">a</div></a>
<a href="#4967"><div id="4966">reliable</div></a>
<a href="#4968"><div id="4967">WiFi-based</div></a>
<a href="#4969"><div id="4968">localization</div></a>
<a href="#4970"><div id="4969">system,</div></a>
<a href="#4971"><div id="4970">and</div></a>
<a href="#4972"><div id="4971">it</div></a>
<a href="#4973"><div id="4972">is</div></a>
<a href="#4974"><div id="4973">very</div></a>
<a href="#4975"><div id="4974">hard</div></a>
<a href="#4976"><div id="4975">to</div></a>
<a href="#4977"><div id="4976">guarantee</div></a>
<a href="#4978"><div id="4977">consistent</div></a>
<a href="#4979"><div id="4978">measurements</div></a>
<a href="#4980"><div id="4979">over</div></a>
<a href="#4981"><div id="4980">time,</div></a>
<a href="#4982"><div id="4981">because</div></a>
<a href="#4983"><div id="4982">the</div></a>
<a href="#4984"><div id="4983">system</div></a>
<a href="#4985"><div id="4984">is</div></a>
<a href="#4986"><div id="4985">highly</div></a>
<a href="#4987"><div id="4986">sensitive</div></a>
<a href="#4988"><div id="4987">to</div></a>
<a href="#4989"><div id="4988">environmental</div></a>
<a href="#4990"><div id="4989">errors.</div></a>
<a href="#4991"><div id="4990">These</div></a>
<a href="#4992"><div id="4991">drawbacks</div></a>
<a href="#4993"><div id="4992">limit</div></a>
<a href="#4994"><div id="4993">the</div></a>
<a href="#4995"><div id="4994">application</div></a>
<a href="#4996"><div id="4995">of</div></a>
<a href="#4997"><div id="4996">WiFi</div></a>
<a href="#4998"><div id="4997">localization</div></a>
<a href="#4999"><div id="4998">system</div></a>
<a href="#5000"><div id="4999">in</div></a>
<a href="#5001"><div id="5000">most</div></a>
<a href="#5002"><div id="5001">public</div></a>
<a href="#5003"><div id="5002">spaces.</div></a>
<a href="#5004"><div id="5003">For</div></a>
<a href="#5005"><div id="5004">example,</div></a>
<a href="#5006"><div id="5005">in</div></a>
<a href="#5007"><div id="5006">2013,</div></a>
<a href="#5008"><div id="5007">the</div></a>
<a href="#5009"><div id="5008">Orlando</div></a>
<a href="#5010"><div id="5009">Airport</div></a>
<a href="#5011"><div id="5010">tried</div></a>
<a href="#5012"><div id="5011">to</div></a>
<a href="#5013"><div id="5012">implement</div></a>
<a href="#5014"><div id="5013">a</div></a>
<a href="#5015"><div id="5014">WiFi-based</div></a>
<a href="#5016"><div id="5015">localization</div></a>
<a href="#5017"><div id="5016">system</div></a>
<a href="#5018"><div id="5017">to</div></a>
<a href="#5019"><div id="5018">help</div></a>
<a href="#5020"><div id="5019">travelers</div></a>
<a href="#5021"><div id="5020">navigate</div></a>
<a href="#5022"><div id="5021">and</div></a>
<a href="#5023"><div id="5022">offer</div></a>
<a href="#5024"><div id="5023">location-based</div></a>
<a href="#5025"><div id="5024">notifications.</div></a>
<a href="#5026"><div id="5025">Unfortunately,</div></a>
<a href="#5027"><div id="5026">a</div></a>
<a href="#5028"><div id="5027">test</div></a>
